/**
132 
 * This class provides an abstract implementation of the visitor that allows its
133 
 * subclasses to scan the metamodel elements by recursively using their
134 
 * (abstract) supertype scanning methods. It declares a scan method for each
135 
 * abstract element of the AST and a visit method for each element of the AST.
136 
 */
137 
public abstract class CtInheritanceScanner implements CtVisitor {
138
139 
	/**
140 
	 * Default constructor.
141 
	 */
142 
	public CtInheritanceScanner() {
143 
	}
144
145 
	public <T> void visitCtCodeSnippetExpression(
146 
			CtCodeSnippetExpression<T> e) {
147 1 1. visitCtCodeSnippetExpression : Removed all instructions in the method → KILLED
 
		scanCtCodeSnippet(e);
148 
		scanCtExpression(e);
149 
		scanCtCodeElement(e);
150 
		scanCtTypedElement(e);
151 
		scanCtElement(e);
152 
		scanCtVisitable(e);
153 
	}
154
155 
	public void visitCtCodeSnippetStatement(CtCodeSnippetStatement e) {
156 1 1. visitCtCodeSnippetStatement : Removed all instructions in the method → KILLED
 
		scanCtCodeSnippet(e);
157 
		scanCtStatement(e);
158 
		scanCtCodeElement(e);
159 
		scanCtElement(e);
160 
		scanCtVisitable(e);
161 
	}
162
163 
	/**
164 
	 * Generically scans a collection of meta-model elements.
165 
	 */
166 
	public void scan(Collection<? extends CtElement> elements) {
167 1 1. scan : Removed all instructions in the method → KILLED
 
		if (elements != null) {
168 
			for (CtElement e : elements) {
169 
				scan(e);
170 
			}
171 
		}
172 
	}
173
174 
	/**
175 
	 * Generically scans a meta-model element.
176 
	 */
177 
	public void scan(CtElement element) {
178 1 1. scan : Removed all instructions in the method → KILLED
 
		if (element != null) {
179 
			element.accept(this);
180 
		}
181 
	}
